< Text>
This would have been a 3 star review, but thanks to stellar customer service (on behalf of our server, John) I couldn't be quicker to change my mind. This was my uncle and I's first visit here and despite being avid restaurant goers, we don't usually bother leaving reviews.

We ordered a large pizza with several toppings, including bacon. It came out undercooked and rubbery which is a "no-go" for my uncle and I. When we brought it to John's attention, he couldn't be more responsive and accommodating. We suggested maybe that he take the bacon that was on the pizza and cook it longer as a means of being more reasonable, but he insisted they make it right and make a new one. He even insisted we keep the 1st pizza for our inconvenience which, even with no bacon, was DELICIOUS! It wasn't too doughy, the ingredients were fresh and they were very generous with the toppings.

We go out to eat almost all the time and we have experienced so many businesses that never bother to weigh to cost of repeat business vs bottom line. I would be thanking my lucky stars as a business owner in an economic climate like this to have an employee like John on their staff to look out for both the business AND the customers alike.

We will most certainly be eating here again and if you value the things I've written above, you ought to as well.<//Text>

<text>I work down the street from this place so it has become a frequent lunch spot for me and coworkers.  Not only is this place delicious but they have a great lunch special.  You can either get two slices of pizza, one topping each, and a soda or one slice of pizza, also one topping, with a salad and a drink for $7.  I always go with the latter so I don't feel so bad about my diet, especially when the slices are enormous.

< Review>
We played Escape Redding‚Äôs ‚ÄúKnight‚Äù room last night and had a good time. There were 6 of us. 2 newbies and 4 of us who have played Escape games at the other Redding Escape Room locations as well as in other cities. The room was done very well. The setting was awesome and all of the props were very cool. I can definitely appreciate the attention to detail that went into creating the experience. The staff member that helped us along our journey was very pleasant.

During our time in the room... 2 of the required props broke. Both were needed to uncover clues to move forward. The staff member had never encountered the issue and was unsure of what to do. It was a little disappointing for us and negatively impacted our experience and forced us to rush at the end to complete the objective.

I would rate my experience as a 3 Star. However, I am happy and supportive of this new local business and hope to see them thrive which is why I am giving it a 4 star rating. <Date>1513917115974</Date>< text>
Oh, Escape Redding is absolutely FANTASTIC and a total must for anyone who loves escape rooms, and/or riddle games!

While I live in the Bay Area now, I grew up in Redding, and never would have imagined that escape rooms would make it this far up North, nor would I have imagined they would be as well thought out as Escape Redding.

A group of nine of us tried our luck with the "Knight Room" and had an incredible time! IT IS SO COOL. The attention to detail in this room is mind boggling - every clue and every riddle is intricately placed. It was challenging enough but not to the point that you were completely frustrated.

Another major plus is how kind the owners are. You can tell they put their heart into this business and thus charge a totally reasonable $25/person. We'll definitely be coming back to try the other rooms next time we're home!< /text>

<Rate>5<//Rate><Review>I will be as honest as possible. I mainly want this review to be seen as a suggestion versus a bad review. We actually had a good time and the staff was friendly. This was the knight.

1. The room where everything is explained before entering the actual room needs to be changed. When I entered this brightly lit room, it took away the suspenseful atmosphere. A bright room just seems like a super happy vibe.
2. In this same room, they used a PowerPoint presentation to explain everything. It kinda felt like being in school, so that too kinda took away the suspenseful vibe. The past host's we've had at different locations were VERY in character and had the script memorized so it felt like we were in an actor's presence. They knew how to set the tone. He was a great guy and all but again, it didn't capture the suspense.
3. There was no background music to help set the tone. No feeling of suspense or the feeling of running out of time. I want my heart racing and i want to be stressing out, lol
4. Another host popped in and out a couple times to help out but it ruined the atmosphere more than anything. When you're at the theater getting lost in the plot, you don't want someone to keep popping in and out, am I right?
5. Some issues with the props. The door was solved by my step dad just by tinkering around with it and not using the clues. That shouldn't be possible. There was a unlocked pad lock that wasn't fastened shut. Host's should double check things like that. There was a missing magnet to complete a task.
6. The tv monitor in the escape room should make like a small beep noise to notify about new information updated on the screen. We get lost in the moment and we don't even think about looking up at the screen.
7. We felt like too many hints had to be given out. The game should make connections quite smoothly. We shouldn't have to depend on the screen. We want to feel that self accomplishment.

We did have fun and I'm open to try another room. I'm not the type to ask for a refund but it would be nice to have a freebie invitation to make up for all the inconveniences that happened that day. Thanks again and I hope this review was helpful.< /Review>< pics>
None<//pics>

Christ Lutheran Church demonstrates that they really care about the community they serve. <Review>The owner and his wife are asian. Their is a little tiny language barrier when you order food in english but it isnt that bad. The owner is really nice. The only thing you have to answer to is combo no combo, everything, and do you want small or large? Personally i think most of the ingrediants are typical over the counter hams and turkeys but the beauty of this place lies in his quality of bread, the size, and all the stuff he jams into the bread. I always order the turkey bacon and cheese. For only $8 this sub is already bursting at the seam but he really loads up on the bacon to top it off. I always question how he makes a profit since bacon is pretty pricey. If you love bread, this is the place for you. The bread is never, and i mean never... stale. you can easily just have half of the sub and eat the other half for dinner. i have been a customer of pj's for about 8 years.< /Review>< Name>

<user>111886051364195072441</user><user_name>Mac<//user_name><time>1579501054691<//time>< rate>
2< /rate>
< Review>
The facility is clean and the owner was very informative and helpful. The Bluetooth stereo system was also an awesome addition.There are however, 2 main drawbacks with this facility.

1. The photos on Google are VERY deceiving. The court is NOT made out of hardwood floors, but instead multiple small tiles that had little air pockets in them. This set-up removed a lot of the bounce from our basketballs and it made dribbling more difficult.

2. The indoor court is incredibly small and the electric box units made it very dangerous for my party to play all out, competitive 5 on 5 basketball. There was even one instance where my friend actually rolled his ankle because of this layout.

Overall the experience was fun, but I probably would not do it again because of the 2 issues listed above. I think the court needs to be renovated/expanded for me to consider this place again-especially for the $50/hour asking price.</Review>

<text>Overall, two thumbs and four paws up!

If you like Pet Food Express, or any other store that feels a lot less like a typical Petco/Petsmart-style huge commercial venture, with gigantic stores and staff that knows very little about what they do, then Unleashed by Petco is for you.

Their product selection is a little less comprehensive than a full-blown Petco, and I think Pet Food Express is far better at stocking well-priced, well-thought-out, and great quality apparel-type items (I always get compliments on my dog's raincoat, which is easily the best thing I never even thought existed, before I saw it at PFE, and even has a functional hood).

That being said, these little stores always seem very thoughtfully stocked, and it's hard to leave this one without a couple large armloads of good quality food (especially if you like the high-quality, grain-free, and high-protein varieties), and necessities that larger stores or other small stores simply don't stock.

This particular store is staffed by really friendly people, and if you own a medium or large dog, you can expect to actually find things here for them, like the dreaded doggie diapers you need to assist your older friend, a large variety of high-quality treats, especially long-lasting and/or puzzle types, and a great selection of hygiene products for fur, skin, teeth, and first aid.  They also carry a basic, but well-chosen and comprehensive range of supplements.  Last but hardly least, this tiny location has a tag engraver, and, of course, the tags to go with it.< /text></record></dataset><record>
